root@b7f2b6d2db5a:/workspace/lgbtqmi# MODEL_ID="${MODEL_ID:-llama-3.1-8b}"
MODEL_PATH="${MODEL_PATH:-/workspace/lgbtqmi/models/llama-3.1-8b}"
DEVICE="${DEVICE:-cuda}"
MAX_ITEMS=2000
# Unique run id (prevents collisions with “today” dirs)
RUN_TAG="rerun-$(date +%H%M%S)"
RUN_DATE="$(date +%F)-max${MAX_ITEMS}-${RUN_TAG}"
RUN_DIR="results/runs/${MODEL_ID}/${RUN_DATE}"
SAE_LOC_DIR="results/sae_localization/${MODEL_ID}/${RUN_DATE}"
SAE_ANALYSIS_DIR="results/sae_analysis/${MODEL_ID}/${RUN_DATE}-logits"
SAE_STEER_DIR="results/sae_steering/${MODEL_ID}/${RUN_DATE}"
SAE_LAYER="${SAE_LAYER:-16}"
SAE_EXPANSION="${SAE_EXPANSION:-32}"
SAE_SOURCE="${SAE_SOURCE:-sae_cache}"
# Ensure datasets
test -d datasets/bbq || git clone https://github.com/nyu-mll/BBQ.git datasets/bbq
test -d datasets/mmlu || hf download --repo-type dataset cais/mmlu --local-dir datasets/mmlu
# Main BBQ pipeline -> results/runs/${MODEL_ID}/${RUN_DATE}
RUN_DATE="${RUN_DATE}" \
MODEL_ID="${MODEL_ID}" \
MODEL_PATH="${MODEL_PATH}" \
DEVICE="${DEVICE}" \
  --max_items "${MAX_ITEMS}"LOC_DIR}" \\y \csv" \/${RUN_DATE}-logits
